###########RUSSIAN DECISIONS###########
###########MVD DECISIONS###########
SOV_mvd_category = {
	SOV_grom_to_rosgvardia = {
		cost = 25
		icon = GFX_decision_sov_grom_button
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_rosguard_start_org
			has_war = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_grom_to_rosgvardia"
			add_to_variable = { SOV_rosgvardia_resistance_growth = -0.10 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_rosgvardia_resistance_damage_to_garrison = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_rosgvardia_police_cost_multiplier_modifier = 0.07 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_rosgvardia3_tt
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 355
		}
	}
	SOV_mobilise_omon = {
		cost = 25
		icon = GFX_decision_sov_omon_button
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_rosguard_start_org
			has_war = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_mobilise_omon"
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } }
				prioritize = { 669 }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"OMON battalion\" division_template = \"Rosgvardia Tank Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.9"
					owner = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 355
		}
	}
	SOV_mobilise_sobr = {

	SOV_separ_povoljie_open = {

	SOV_anti_tatar_separ = {
		cost = 50
		icon = GFX_decision_sovmvd_tv_button
		days_remove = 80
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = SUB_separ_povoljie_open
			TAT = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = SUB_subject_rebeliion_flag }
				OR = {
					SOV = { owns_state = 661 }
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_republic_rf
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_kray_rf
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_oblast_rf
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_okrug_rf
				}
			}
			check_variable = { TAT.subjectinped > 1 }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_anti_tatar_separ"
			TAT = {
				set_temp_variable = { modify_subjectinped = -4 }
				modify_subjectinped_support = yes
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 355
		}
	}

# Cooperation with Taiwan
SOV_democracy_taiwam_category = {
	SOV_boost_opinion_of_rus = {
		cost = 25
		icon = GFX_decision_taiwan_export
		days_remove = 150
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			country_exists = TAI
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_Cooperation_with_Taiwan
				has_completed_focus = SOV_expand_trade_with_taiwan
			}
			TAI = {
				OR = {
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
				western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
				western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 355 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_boost_opinion_of_rus"
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = TAI
				modifier = recent_actions_positive
			}
			TAI = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SOV
					modifier = recent_actions_positive
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TAI }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}
	SOV_more_weapon_taiwan = {
		cost = 45
		icon = GFX_decision_taiwan_export
		days_remove = 220
		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			country_exists = TAI
			has_completed_focus = SOV_support_taiwan_military_buildup

				OR = {
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV }
				}
			}

				western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
				western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
				western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
			}

	SOV_npp_ticker_mission = {
		available = { always = no }
		activation = { has_completed_focus = SOV_npp }
		days_mission_timeout = 800
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		icon = GFX_decision_npp_button
		cancel_trigger = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_npp_completion_trigger_TT
				OR = {
					check_variable = { npp_completed = 5 }
					check_variable = { npp_completed > 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = { check_variable = { npp_completed < 5 } }
		cancel_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.12
			country_event = { id = russia.27 days = 1 }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.12
			add_political_power = -100
			country_event = { id = russia.26 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	SOV_npp_healthcare = {
		cost = 90
		icon = none
		days_remove = 365
		fire_only_once = yes
		icon = GFX_decision_npp_button
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.01
			monthly_population = 0.05
			stability_factor = 0.01
			health_cost_multiplier_modifier = 0.05
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 355 }
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_npp_healthcare"
			add_stability = 0.06
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			add_to_variable = {
				var = npp_completed
				value = 1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_npp_healthcare_tt
			add_to_variable = { SOV_npp_health_cost = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_npp_population = 0.03 }
		}
	}

SOV_bars_category = {
	SOV_first_bars_start = {
		cost = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_bars1_button
		days_remove = 55
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { factor = 355 }
		available = {
			has_war = yes
			owns_state = 668
			owns_state = 1140
		}
		visible = {	has_completed_focus = SOV_form_bars	}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_first_bars_start"
			add_manpower = -4000
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -3 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
					has_country_flag = SOV_wagner_parties
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.005 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } }
				prioritize = { 668 }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"BARS-1\" division_template = \"BARS Battalion\" start_experience_factor = 0.7"

				}
			}
		}

	SOV_reunification_mission = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }
		fire_only_once = no
		is_good = yes
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 29 # becomes 30 with refire

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission SOV_reunification_mission"

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { reunification_progress > 99 }
				}

				country_event = { id = sov_dissolution.2 days = 1 }
				var:THIS.reunification_target = {
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
					}
				}

				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = reunification_strains_idea
					days = 365
				}

				clear_variable = reunification_target
				clear_variable = reunification_progress
				clr_country_flag = reunification_talks_in_progress
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					30 = { country_event = { id = sov_dissolution.10 days = 1 } }
					20 = { country_event = { id = sov_dissolution.11 days = 1 } }
					10 = { country_event = { id = sov_dissolution.12 days = 1 } }
				}

				hidden_effect = {
					add_to_variable = { reunification_progress = 5 }
					activate_mission = SOV_reunification_mission
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
SOV_space_shuttle_category = {
	SOV_buran_hangar = {
		activation = {
			original_tag = SOV
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_mission_space_ended
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_country_flag = SOV_mission_space_ended
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 862

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout SOV_buran_hangar"
			country_event = {
				id = russia.302
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout SOV_buran_hangar"
			set_country_flag = SOV_failed_mission
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SOV_funding_success
				}
				country_event = {
					id = russia.303
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = russia.304
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Decisions
	SOV_begin_funding = {

		icon = GFX_decision_buran_button

		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 30

		available = {
			check_variable = { treasury > 9.9 }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { treasury > 9.9 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = cost_10_0

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = SOV_failed_mission
					has_country_flag = SOV_funding_success
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_begin_funding"
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = paralyzing_corruption
						has_idea = crippling_corruption
						has_idea = rampant_corruption
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.300
						}
					}
					20 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.200
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_funding_fail_likely_TT
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = unrestrained_corruption
					has_idea = systematic_corruption
					has_idea = widespread_corruption
				}
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.300
						}
					}
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.200
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_funding_might_fail_TT
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = medium_corruption
					has_idea = modest_corruption
					has_idea = slight_corruption
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.300
						}
					}
					80 = {
						country_event = {
							id = russia.200
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_funding_could_fail_TT
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = negligible_corruption
				}
				country_event = {
					id = russia.200
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_funding_success_TT
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			tax_gain_multiplier_modifier = -0.10
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
	}

		 	has_country_flag = SOV_made_repairs
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_announce_full_restoration"
			country_event = {
				id = russia.302
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.301
			}
			set_country_flag = SOV_mission_space_ended
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
	}
